    FROM `Article_commentUser_account` AS `a`

    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM `Article_commentUser_account1` AS `a1`
    INNER JOIN `Accounts` AS `a2` ON `a1`.`Users_who_dislikedId` = `a2`.`Id`
    WHERE (`c`.`Id` = `a1`.`Article_comment1Id`) AND (`c`.`Article_id` = `a1`.`Article_comment1Article_id`))
